Tang Zongguo Reports on the Tragic Situation of the Disaster in Huoqiu and Other Counties 108

Bandit Drought for Seven Years...Bark Stripped...Extremely Heavy Disaster...Awaiting Relief with Utmost Urgency, Hundreds of Starving People...Women Sold in Human Markets...Soup Kitchens Maintain the Status Quo. Tang Zongguo, Director of Anhui Urgent Relief of the Shanghai Fundraising Association for Water Disasters in Various Provinces, telegraphed the association yesterday: To Mr. Cheng Yiqing of the Shanghai Fundraising Association for Water Disasters in Various Provinces and all benefactors: Huoqiu and other counties have suffered from bandit droughts for seven years, and the reserves have been exhausted for a long time. The drought last year was particularly severe, with no harvest. Starving people are seen on the roads every day. The surviving people are thin and weak, as if about to fall in the wind. Those selling women, doors, windows, and furniture are seen on the roads. The bark of elm trees along the roads has been stripped bare. Where our colleagues inspected the disaster in person, more than 100 people starved to death in one district of Lianhua Temple, more than 70 people starved to death in one district of Changtang Shao, and more than 200 people starved to death or were sold in one district of He Kouji. There are human markets in Gaotang Town, Sanhejian, and other places, where women sit in rows for sale. The government strictly prohibits this, but cannot stop it. The tragic situation is unprecedented, except for the Shaanxi disaster in 1929. We will first allocate 20,000 yuan from the Relief Committee to Huoqiu for inspection and release to alleviate the urgent situation. However, it is a drop in the bucket and difficult to provide comprehensive relief. The wheat harvest will be more than two months away. Even if we provide one yuan per person, it is difficult to extend it until the wheat ripens. Those who do not receive relief are uncountable. The county officials and gentry in the city have set up a soup kitchen with a limit of 1,200 people receiving soup, which is quite effective. We are now planning to persuade them to set up soup kitchens in Wulong Temple, He Kouji, Sanliuji, Panji, and Yejiji to prolong their lives and supplement the inspections that have not been completed. We have allocated 5,000 yuan, but we do not know where it has been remitted. We will use this money to subsidize six soup kitchens in Huoqiu. Please instruct us to comply. The lottery ticket is worth 10,000 yuan. Please do your best to support it and make a decision on relieving Anhui as soon as possible, and ask the bank to borrow cash to facilitate inspection and release. Once we receive a definite indication, we will dispatch to Shouzhou and other counties for inspection and release. Mr. Li Tianzhen has gone to Hefei for inspection and release. Please keep this in mind. Guo is currently in the Corruption Property Committee and hereby reports. Tang Zongguo bows and sings.

The Sauce and Wine Industry Rectifies Industry Rules and Fines are Donated to Aviation for National Salvation 109

The products sold in the sauce and wine industry are essential for people's daily life. Therefore, the industry's shops are located throughout the streets and alleys. Five years ago, statistics showed that there were more than 2,500 shops in the city. In recent years, due to the impact of the economic downturn and the infighting among the industry, those with weak capital have been squeezed out. Currently, there are only more than 2,000 shops left in the city, and only a few can make a profit at the end of the year. Zhang Dalian and Han Xingwei, members of the Shanghai Sauce and Wine Industry Association, in view of this, publicly formulated industry rules in 1933. In June of the same year, they were approved by the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau for implementation, and earnestly rectified the industry. However, over time, people became lazy, and a few industry members still disobeyed in secret. The association convened a general meeting of members in February of this year, and after strict discussion, decided to implement the industry rules, dividing the city into five districts, each district divided into several groups, and elected group leaders. The group leaders mutually elected district leaders. The association hired Liu Dingji as the general director, and negotiated with the Aviation Association for approval. If anyone deliberately violates the industry rules, the penalties will be determined according to the industry rules and sent to the Aviation Association, which will then request the Public Security Bureau to enforce them, and the money will be donated to the Aviation for National Salvation. The industry rules state that all industry members should join the association. The concession is also preparing a proper solution. The South District will start investigating on April 1st and gradually extend to other districts. It is believed that the sauce and wine industry will be rectified. It is also heard that the association's market quotation sheets are difficult to distribute due to the large area of the city. It has now negotiated with various newspapers to add sauce and wine industry market quotations in the economic news.

The Wang Luo Abandonment Lawsuit 110

Raising a Son in the Flying Snow on New Year's Eve. Nothing Happened After Meeting at the Dance Hall

Luo Sen, 29 years old, from Siyang, owner of the Sen Sen Chemical Glass Factory at No. 17 Tailai Lane, Maigen Road, previously cohabited with Wang Qinhua (21 years old), a woman from Changzhou, in the Ruihua Rice Cake Shop in Baoxing Lane, Baoxing Road, Zhabei. Last New Year's Eve, she gave birth to a son. Because it was snowing heavily at that time, he was named Xuesheng. At that time, Luo paid Wang 150 yuan per month for living expenses. Now that Luo has a new love, he abandoned Wang, causing Wang to hire lawyers Ling Qihong and Liu Liang to file a criminal lawsuit with the First Special District Court based on Article 229 and Article 294 of the Criminal Law, which pertain to offenses against morality. Luo Sen, on the other hand, claimed that Wang was a dancer in the former Liangyou Dance Hall and that they met through dancing. He admits that Wang's allegations are true. Yesterday morning, Feng Shide, the chief judge of the criminal court of the First Special District Court, summoned Luo Sen and his lawyer to court. After Feng inquired about his age and origin, he announced that the hearing was adjourned because the case concerned morality and bystanders were prohibited.

Triangular Love: Two Men Stir Up Trouble in the Sea of Jealousy 111

Shen Deming Suffers Serious Head Injuries, Shi Jimin's Face is Also Scratched

Shi Jimin, 23 years old, from Nanjing, and Shen Deming, 22 years old, live near Singapore Road in West Shanghai, but they are not acquainted. Shi Jimin likes to flirt and had an affair with Da Genzi, a woman from the Yunji Barber Shop at No. 584 Xiaoshadu Road. Unexpectedly, Shen Deming is also an idler who wanders around all day. He accidentally saw Shi's lover and was struck by her beauty. The woman is also fickle, and they flirted with each other. Soon, Shen was also able to become a guest in her boudoir. However, the affair was not secret and was discovered by Shi. Therefore, Shi ambushed near the intersection of Xiaoshadu Road and Singapore Road yesterday afternoon. When Shen Deming passed by, he confronted him. The two sides disagreed and started fighting. However, Shen was no match for Shi. His head was beaten and he suffered the most serious injuries, collapsing on the side of the road. Shi's face was also scratched a little by Shen's fingers. The incident was noticed by a police officer, who rushed to the scene and took both parties to the police station for investigation. Shen Deming's injuries were serious, and he was transferred to the hospital for treatment.

Attempted Rape of a Widow After Enticement: Wang Pan Has No Place to Appeal 112

Wang Pan, a young widow living in Jingxing Lane, No. 2 Aiwunyi Road in the British Concession, is in her thirties and has some wealth. She has been a widow for six years and hires Xu Zhao from Yangzhou as a servant. Yan Zhaoying (living at No. 58 Chuaxinhe Bridge), who has known her for a long time, coveted her. At noon on the 9th of this month, he suddenly went to Wang Pan's house, falsely claiming that he had a quarrel with his wife and wanted Wang Pan to go and mediate. She was unaware of his plan and went with him. Unexpectedly, Yan Zhaoying led her to the Anle Inn on Sanyangjing Bridge, where he closed the door and used coercive and violent means to attempt to rape her. She resisted desperately and escaped. After returning home, she tried to commit suicide but was dissuaded by the servant and roommate. However, she was unwilling to submit. The day before yesterday morning, she took her servant to the city and turned Yan Zhaoying over to the Lao Beimen Police Station for investigation. After interrogation, there was no corroborating evidence, and the case occurred in the French Concession. She was instructed to file a lawsuit with the French Concession Court.

A Matchmaker Abducts and Conceals a Married Woman 113

Li Zhang is Weak-Willed, What is Wu Zhenlong's Intention?

Li Chaofeng, 22 years old, from Hebei, was a police officer in Beiping and was very capable. Therefore, he was highly valued by the Beiping police chief. After the January 28th Incident, the city made great efforts to reorganize the police force and transferred capable police officers from Beiping and Tianjin to Shanghai. Li was one of them and was assigned to the Linping Road Police Station of the North Station Branch. In November of last year, Li, through the mediation of Wu Zhenlong (41 years old), a carpenter from Nantong who lives at No. 51 Yuhua Lane, Tianbao Road, Zhabei, married Zhang, a woman from Changzhou. After the marriage, the relationship between the couple was harmonious and they enjoyed each other's company. A month ago, Li received an order to go to the First Phase Police Concentration Training Team for training. When Li returned home after completing the training, he suddenly learned that Zhang had disappeared. He immediately searched everywhere but found no clues. It was not until about 10:00 AM yesterday that he found her at the home of the matchmaker, Wu Zhenlong. Li believed that Wu was suspected of abducting and concealing her. He immediately twisted him into the police station. After the police station briefly interrogated them, the case involved allegations of abducting and concealing a woman, which was a criminal case. Therefore, they prepared a document and sent all three defendants to the General Bureau for interrogation.

The Xinzha Branch Detective Team Cracked the Escape and Theft of Lu Ronghua and Others 114

Lu Ronghua, who had accumulated thefts, stole property in Pingmin Village, Pushan Road, Zhabei, around 8:00 PM on the 1st of this month. He was arrested by Wang Zufufu, the director of Pingmin Village Housing Management, and sent to the Tanmiaoqiao Police Station for interrogation. The thief took advantage of the inattentiveness of the guarding police officer, Song Jinghui, and escaped without a trace. Later, the Xinzha Branch sent police officer Song to the Public Security Bureau for punishment. He has not been released yet. A few days later, Detective Sun Youzhi of the Xinzha Detective Team suddenly received a tip that the escaped thief Lu Ronghua and others were hiding at No. 19 Guoqing Road and so on. Detective Sun immediately reported to the chief and deputy captains and dispatched squad leader Li Shouchang, leading the original detectives Sun Youzhi, Zhong Yun, Zhang Shuwen, Xiao Huaiyu, and others to go there. They separately captured Lu and his accomplice Zhang Gaojin (also known as Xiao Ningbo) and copied out stolen goods and weapons. After being brought back to the team, the two thieves confessed that in addition to stealing property from Pingmin Village, Pushan Road on the evening of the 1st of this month, they had previously committed many crimes at No. 38 Chongde Lane, Hengfeng Road and other places in the Chinese Concession. After the team verified the confession, they transferred the thieves Lu Ronghua (aka Jin Sheng), 27 years old, from Ningbo, Zhang Gaojin (aka Xiao Ningbo), 24 years old, also from Ningbo, together with the stolen goods and weapons to the Xinzha Branch and then to the Public Security Bureau for distribution yesterday.

Fire at Dabeitex Factory, West Baoxing Road 118

Fire Started in the Drying Room, Losses Exceed a Thousand Gold Pieces

The Dabeitex Factory in Sanyang Lane, West Baoxing Road, Zhabei, is owned and operated by Ningbo native Wang Changquan, and its business is relatively prosperous. At about 3:20 PM yesterday, a fire broke out in the factory's drying room, ignited by the flammability of the cloth. The fire blazed up instantly, piercing through the roof and threatening to spread widely. Fortunately, various fire brigades rushed to the scene with water pumps and extinguished the fire after some time. It is estimated that two bungalows and cloth were destroyed by the fire, resulting in losses exceeding a thousand gold pieces. The factory's accountant, Zhang Ruyuan from Taixing (35 years old, residing at No. 66 Sanyang Road), was arrested by the police dispatched from the West Baoxing Road Police Station and taken to the North Station Branch Bureau for interrogation.

Huining Fellow Townsmen Association's Dispute Over Commercial Rights Regarding the Wutun Road Route 119

Yesterday, the Huining Fellow Townsmen Association in Shanghai researched the dispute over the northeastern and southwestern routes of the Wutun Highway. A telegram was sent to Director Liu of the Anhui Construction Department, Commissioner Shi of Xiuning, and County Magistrate Chen of Wuyuan. The original telegram stated: "Since the proposal to build the Tunwu Highway, both Wuxiu counties have sent personnel to survey and actively proceed. This is good news. However, recently, people from the two counties have been mutually contesting the northeastern and southwestern routes, each sticking to their own opinion and unable to reach a decision. Our association believes that this issue is greatly related to the prosperity of the entire Huizhou and the development of transportation. Furthermore, it is important for the convenience of suppressing remnant bandits. The matter is important and should not be viewed from only one perspective. We should weigh the pros and cons fairly and discuss it calmly, so that it can be completed as soon as possible. We have consulted familiar fellow townsmen regarding the terrain of Wuxiu and the essential points of commercial transportation, and considered them to serve as an accurate balance. However, according to the majority of opinions, Wuyuan's massive production of tea and various goods has always been concentrated in Jiangwan, exported via Longwan in Xiunan. Other goods such as salt and kerosene are also imported via Longwan to reach the entire Wuyuan. Carrying goods on shoulders and backs fills the roads. Taking the highway through Wudong, via Longwan in Xiunan to Tunxi, would not only be convenient for travelers, but also greatly facilitate commercial transportation. Furthermore, from the perspective of suppressing remnant bandits, the majority advocate using the eastern route. If one takes the western route through the Qinhua Boundary and Jieshou in Beixiang to connect with the Tunjing Road Post, it is not only inconsistent in name but also seems far-fetched. To make a fair judgment, the eastern route is still preferable. In conclusion, for the sake of both counties' transportation interests, it is best to adopt the majority's opinion as the decision. Be impartial and let it be completed as soon as possible. Do not obstruct the progress of the road due to disputes over route benefits. Therefore, we earnestly request that Your Excellency accept the majority's public opinion, consider the overall situation, and resolutely decide to order the engineers to conduct surveys and construction to benefit the transportation of both counties and create benefits for the local area. We await your orders anxiously. The Huining Fellow Townsmen Association in Shanghai bows."

It has received support from all sectors of society and is now located at No. 451, at the intersection of North Jiangxi Road and Old Baizi Road in Hongkou, in a three-story building. World Games Track and Field Preliminary Selection: Shen Siliang and Others Decide in Beiping, to be Held in Shanghai at the End of May 124

An International Track and Field Meet Will Also Be Held, Training Begins in Beiping on the 16th of this Month

(Special Dispatch from Beiping) Shen Siliang, the executive director of the Chinese National Amateur Athletic Federation, arrived in Beiping by train from Shanghai on the morning of the 9th. Those welcoming him at the station included John Ma, Dong Shouyi, Zhao Yunxie, and several others. After arriving in Beiping, Shen took a car to Dong Shouyi's residence for lunch. After the meal, Shen, Dong, and Ma held a meeting at Dong's residence to discuss the training of athletes to participate in the World Games. After the meeting, Shen inspected the basketball team's training situation. On the 9th and 10th, he made statements to reporters. On the 11th, Shen went to Tianjin to meet with Zhang Boling to discuss matters related to participating in the World Games. He is scheduled to return to Shanghai by train that night. Details of the situation in various aspects are listed below.

Shen Discusses Methods for Going to Germany 125

Shen told reporters at Tsinghua University that the football team has decided to select 22 players. After the selection, they will go to Shanghai for training on the 23rd of this month. On the 2nd of next month, the football team will embark on a journey to Southeast Asia, competing in over 20 matches. After the matches, they will not return to China but will go to London, England, to board a ship with the Chinese delegation to the World Games and travel to Germany to attend the World Games. Yang Xiuqiong and Guo Zhenheng are considered to be promising swimming athletes. The performance of the other two is still under detailed review. The list will be announced in early June. The track and field association has been entrusted to select one representative for the walking race in Shanghai. Due to budget constraints, it is difficult to accommodate the request to send one more person. Yan Chengkun has been appointed as the football coach. Boxing athletes have been training in Shanghai recently with excellent results. The training steps are progressing from basic methods. This month, there will be a friendly match with Westerners in Shanghai. Germany's preparations for the Games have been exceptionally active recently. The rumors of postponement are likely speculations. The summer training courses and discussions will not be held this year. These three events were originally supposed to be organized by the Ministry of Education. The Standing Committee will convene again this month to discuss various methods for participating in the World Games, methods for centralized training of athletes, and other issues that need to be decided for the trip. A full board meeting may not be held again. If necessary, the third full board meeting will be held in Shanghai before the athletes leave the country. In addition to the 20 members of the association and the Ministry of Education who will go to Germany to observe sports, there may be several people who will travel at their own expense to visit with the delegation, but they must also have the appropriate qualifications.

Key Points of the Giant's Meeting 126

Shen held a meeting at Dong Shouyi's residence, attended by John Ma, Shen Siliang, and Dong Shouyi. The following cases were passed: How to stipulate the training of representatives of our country attending the World Games in Beiping. Resolved: (A) Track and field preliminary selection athletes will begin training in Beiping on the 16th of this month for a period of 40 days. After training, they can participate in the preliminary selection. (B) Registration will begin immediately and close on the 16th. The registration location is the National Sports Advancement Association in Shanghai. The participation standards will be formulated by Ma Dehan. (C) Participants in the training will bear their own travel expenses, and the Athletic Association will bear the cost of food and lodging. (D) Shen Siliang, John Ma, and Dong Shouyi will contact the Tsinghua University authorities to arrange venues and dormitories. The case of the preliminary selection of track and field representatives for the World Games. Resolved: (A) The preliminary selection will be held in Shanghai on May 30th and 31st. (B) The number of selected people is determined to be 12. (C) The National Sports Association will host the International Track and Field Competition in Shanghai to select from among them. The case of the selection of swimming representatives. Resolved: It was decided not to hold a swimming preliminary selection. Only those with particularly excellent results from Hong Kong, Guangdong, and Shanghai will be selected. The number of people has not yet been determined. The case of the date of the basketball team's training in Beiping. Resolved: The training period will be two months, ending on June 14th. They will leave Beiping for Shanghai on that day to concentrate and prepare to set sail for overseas on the 26th. The case of following the delegation to the World Games to Germany to observe sports personnel. Resolved: (A) The number of qualified personnel will be determined after the registration deadline. (B) The Ministry of Education has female participants registering, but the German Sports Association stipulates that it is limited to males. Females are not qualified to enter the venue for observation and can only observe the situation from the outside. Our country has also decided to comply with this. (C) The Athletic Association will select one person to guide the observation policy. The selection of personnel is pending. The meeting adjourned at 3:00 PM.

Municipal Education Bureau Schedules Municipal Elementary School Games 130

Dates: May 14-16 Location: Municipal Sports Field in the City Center

In order to promote the physical fitness of elementary school students in the city and to examine the physical education achievements of the elementary schools, the Municipal Education Bureau has stipulated that the joint elementary school sports meet will be held for three days in the spring of each year. The previous joint elementary school sports meet was divided into eight districts in the city in order to promote the physical education of various schools in the city, and the results were satisfactory. However, the results were not able to be compared because the results of each district were excellent. This year, it was decided to follow the educational administrative district regulations and hold preliminary meetings by district first (the educational administrative districts total 22 districts, but it was decided that the downtown area and Yinhang district will be held jointly, Yinxiang district and Jiangwan district will be held jointly, and Luru district and Pengpu district will be held jointly, for a total of 19 districts). Each district will hold a preliminary selection in advance to select representatives, and then attend the city-wide joint sports meet. It is heard that the date of the joint sports meet has been set for May 14-16 and will be held at the municipal sports field in the city center for three consecutive days. According to the examples of previous sessions, it will be divided into male and female groups A, B, and C. Weight will be measured according to the regulations of the previous session, but the maximum weight of group A must not exceed 105 pounds. In other words, athletes in group A who weigh 105 pounds or more will be classified as a performance group. The preliminary selection dates for each district must be completed by the end of April. Registration for each district must be submitted to the conference by May 5. Late registrations will not be accepted. If the registration form is not completed according to the regulations, it will not be assigned. All rules and other documents will be announced soon.

Education News

Ministry of Education Dispatches Revised Senior High School Physical Education Curriculum Standards (Part 1) 133

First, Objectives

Continuing from the above: To cultivate personality, enable sound physical and mental development, nurture the sports skills needed in life, emphasize group sports, continue training civic morality, correct poor posture in physical development, and develop a habit of using sports as recreation.

Second, Time Allocation

Regular class time: two hours per week. Morning exercises, recess exercises, and extracurricular sports are held outside of regular class time.

Third, Textbook Outline

First Academic Year: 1. Gymnastics; 2. Apparatus exercise; 3. Group mixed apparatus exercises; 4. Track and field (reduced for girls, armed running added for boys, applicable teaching materials such as hand grenades); 5. Ball sports; 6. Outdoor activities (including swimming, skating, mountain climbing, riding, rowing, and others), use as much as possible outside of class; 7. Traditional Chinese martial arts (in addition to emphasizing the use of knives, spears, swords, and clubs, add items such as stone weights, stone locks, and attack and defense methods); 8. Dance (reduced for boys); 9. Games; 10. Corrective exercises (for those with physical defects); 11. Gentle exercise (selected by those unsuitable for strenuous exercise).

Second Academic Year: 1. Gymnastics; 2. Apparatus exercise; 3. Track and field (reduced for girls, armed running and throwing hand grenades added for boys, applicable teaching materials); 4. Ball sports; 5. Outdoor activities (including swimming, skating, mountain climbing, riding, rowing, and others), use as much as possible outside of class; 6. Traditional Chinese martial arts (in addition to emphasizing the use of knives, spears, swords, and clubs, add items such as stone weights, stone locks, and attack and defense methods); 7. Dance (reduced for boys); 8. Games; 9. Corrective exercises (for those with physical defects); 10. Gentle exercise (selected by those unsuitable for strenuous exercise). Third Academic Year: 1. Gymnastics; 2. Apparatus exercise; 3. Track and field (reduced for girls, armed running and throwing hand grenades added for boys, applicable teaching materials); 4. Ball sports; 5. Outdoor activities (including swimming, skating, mountain climbing, riding, rowing, and others), use as much as possible outside of class; 6. Traditional Chinese martial arts (in addition to emphasizing the use of knives, spears, swords, and clubs, add items such as stone weights, stone locks, and attack and defense methods); 7. Dance (reduced for boys); 8. Games; 9. Corrective exercises (for those with physical defects); 10. Gentle exercise (selected by those unsuitable for strenuous exercise). (Note) If weather conditions prevent outdoor classes, lectures on physical education knowledge and sports rules can be given indoors.

Fourth, Summary of Implementation Methods

Work Items:

1. Regular classes; 2. Morning exercises; 3. Extracurricular sports; 4. Organization of various extracurricular activities: (A) Intra-school competitions; (B) Inter-school competitions; (C) Excursions and trips; (D) Various designs and performances.

Key Teaching Points

Regarding senior high school physical education teaching methods, in addition to the principles of junior high school, attention should be paid to leadership training to prepare students to lead social sports after leaving school. The key teaching points are listed below: 1. Apply as much as possible the complete learning method and analytical learning method of ordinary teaching methods, as well as the law of readiness, law of exercise, and law of effect of educational psychology.

2. Regular classes, morning exercises, and extracurricular sports should be interconnected to avoid repetition and student boredom. (A) Regular classes should focus on basic training and the teaching of methods and rules for each sport. The teacher's work is heavier. (B) Extracurricular sports should focus on students' actual practice. At this time, the teacher is only responsible for management. (C) Morning exercises or recess activities should focus on gentle physical activity, and their function is to regulate life, with natural activities as the main focus. 3. Adopt group competition methods as much as possible, pay attention to universal sports, and avoid the competition system of a few athletes. 4. Hold skill tests at least once per semester. At the beginning of the semester, announce the test methods in advance to encourage students to work hard in practice. 5. Traditional Chinese martial arts should focus on application. 6. Schools without indoor sports facilities should make full use of ordinary indoor facilities for special sports activities. 7. Sanitary facilities, such as bathrooms, should be fully equipped. 8. According to the environment of each school, formulate various standards for skills, health, and common sense. 9. Use holidays to create large group sports design activities, such as celebrations and joint sports meets. 10. Unite with other groups in sports to compare and promote progress. 11. Conduct health checks of all students within three weeks after the start of each school year. 12. Adopt ability grouping methods as much as possible. Physical education grading cannot be based on general intelligence. Because students of different regions are of different ages and have different degrees of physical development, students of the same grade may not be suitable for the same type of teaching materials. Therefore, ability grouping should be adopted as much as possible within the scope of possibility. In addition to the grade level, the following five types should be used as standards (see appendix). 13. Gymnastics (using basic movements of ball sports, track and field, and apparatus exercises for analytical practice as preparation for various sports).

Appendix: Grading Methods

In addition to the original grade division method, divide into the following five types: 1. Gender; 2. Results of physical examination; 3. Age, height, and weight; 4. Physical fitness; 5. Skills. The five types of grading methods are briefly explained below: 1. Gender: After the age of twelve or thirteen, boys and girls develop differently and have different interests. Therefore, physical education in ordinary senior high schools should be taught in completely separate classes. 2. Results of health examination: Health examination is one of the most important events in school administration. At least one examination should be conducted for each student every year. The results of the examination should be used as a reference for physical education grading. Students with poor physical development or defects should be given special instruction. 3. Age, height, and weight: Students of different ages and with different development are difficult to teach together in physical education classes. Many schools use age, height, and weight for grading, some use only one type, some use two types in combination, and some use three types in combination, with the combination of three being the best. McCloy's athletic skills standard score table can be used for application. A simple method is listed below for application and can still be changed during use. As shown in the table, it is divided into seven levels. During application, the index obtained by senior high school students can be divided into two or three levels according to the actual situation.

Ministry of Education Actively Promotes Free Education Measures 134

Each Local Area is Divided into Elementary School Districts; Rural Teachers and Principals are Concentrated for Training

(Nanjing, 11th) The Ministry of Education announced more than ten resolutions of the National Free Education Committee on the 11th. The more important ones include (regarding free education funding): Resolutions: The detailed amount of fundraising in each local area must be submitted to the ministry for record. The annual free education funding to be raised by each province and city should be included in the formal budget, and the same applies to each county and city. (Regarding educational administration): Resolutions: Each local area must be uniformly divided into elementary school districts within this year. Each district must have at least one short-term elementary school, and the county mayor and school board are responsible for implementing reward and punishment measures. At the end of this year, the responsible officials who have effectively implemented free education will be rewarded. (Regarding free education teachers): Resolutions: The central government will concentrate on training educational administrative personnel in one county or city to promote the rapid advancement of free education, and the country will be divided into several inspection areas, with inspections assigned by the ministry and departments. Starting from the next year, the central government will concentrate on training rural teachers and principals, 500 to 600 people each year, with a training period of one year. Starting from the 26th year, rural normal schools will be established in each county, aiming to achieve at least one rural teacher in each county within three years, so that the qualifications of free education teachers across the country tend to be consistent.

(Central News Agency, Nanjing, 11th) The National Free Education Committee held a meeting on the 8th and passed a resolution, which the Ministry of Education announced on the 11th: (A) Regarding free education funding: The detailed items and amounts of fundraising in each local area will be determined by the ministry, and a form will be issued to report in detail for record. For the next year, the free education funds to be raised by each province and city should be submitted to the Executive Yuan to order each province and city to be included in the 25th year budget and paid from the normal income of each province and city. The fees to be raised by each county and city should be notified to each province and city to instruct each county and city to include the newly added free education fees in the 25th year budget and detail the funding methods. (B) Regarding free education administration: Each local book should be divided into elementary school districts and uniformly divided within this year. Each district should have at least one short-term elementary school, and its funding should be based on self-raising by each joint guarantee or elementary school district. Poor districts may be subsidized by the central government and provinces. Each district should immediately establish a school board to handle district affairs, and the county magistrate should formulate reward and punishment measures for the school board and implement them at the end of each year. The ministry will formulate reward and punishment measures for county magistrates for handling free education, and at the end of this year, each education department will assess and report to the ministry, and submit it to the Executive Yuan for rewards and punishments respectively, and implement the resolution within this year. The above four proposals were passed. The responsible officials who have effectively implemented free education this year will be submitted by the ministry to the Executive Yuan for rewards at the end of the year. (C) Regarding free education teachers: Educational administrative personnel in each county and city should be centrally trained by the central government in batches. The country will be divided into several inspection areas, with inspections assigned by the ministry and provincial inspectors. Provincial inspectors should live in the designated area. Starting from the 25th year, the central government will concentrate on training rural normal school principals, 500 to 600 people each year, with a period of one year. Starting from the 26th year, rural teachers will be established in each county, aiming to achieve at least one rural teacher in each county within three years. Resolutions: The above proposals were passed in principle, and the ministry will detail the training methods, as well as the ministry inspector and provincial inspector's district inspection methods.

Even if it can be predicted, it cannot be determined. For the sake of national security, we should seek more welfare for mankind. It is worth thinking deeply about and planning for a long time. I believe that the gains and losses of our school in the next forty years depend on how we work hard. The following four major issues must not be ignored: How can we make the talents we create meet the needs, so that the name and reality can be consistent? How can we make the prepared personnel transform the environment, so that groups and individuals can coexist? Can we feel the expectations of society and can we promote our responsibilities? Can we value the honor of alumni and can we take on our responsibilities?

Ten Important Aspects of Vocational Supplementary Education (Part 3) 142

— Jiang Wenyu

(9)

Let's take a look at the general workers. We can never say that most workers don't have outstanding geniuses, because there are too many people, so there must be special people. These special geniuses are already very wronged because they have no ability to go to school. If there is no opportunity for supplementary education for them, isn't that even more unfair to them? I am very confident that if there are vocational supplementary schools at all levels to provide them with training, a part of these special geniuses will definitely be able to show themselves, stand out, and become great talents. Unfortunately, a group of old-fashioned agricultural, industrial, and commercial circles have buried many geniuses because they have no supplementary education. This is really very important. This is seeing the importance of vocational supplementary education from the perspective of special geniuses.

(10)

There is one more point that I want to add. All undertakings in the world should be valued for their economy. If you can use less cost and have greater effectiveness, then the value of success is relatively high. Ordinary education requires building school buildings, purchasing instruments, buying specimens, and various equipment, which costs a lot. As a result, a lot of material resources are consumed, and the actual results may not be as expected. Moreover, in terms of equipment, it may not be fully utilized. This is so regrettable. If vocational supplementary schools can borrow existing school buildings and existing instruments and specimens without additional equipment, and the educational goals have been achieved, it would be much more convenient to set up supplementary schools in farms and factories. Then, since there are formal schools and other farms and factories that can be used, why not do it? Moreover, this method is beneficial to all parties. Schools, farms, and factories can get a lot of help with supplementary schools, and supplementary schools can be set up in many places without additional equipment. Isn't this very economical? Moreover, I hope that in the future, vocational supplementary schools can be set up in all public places. This is seeing the importance of vocational supplementary education from the perspective of convenience and economic effectiveness.

Now that vocational supplementary education has these ten important aspects, shouldn't we greatly promote it, greatly advocate it, and greatly popularize it? (The End)

Research on Anhui Tea (4) 155

— Shi Jifa

(V) Opinions on the Improvement of Anhui Tea

Anhui tea, struggling on the brink of death, is primarily facing a sharp decline in production due to abandoned tea gardens, bankrupt tea merchants (suffering losses), and a desolate tea market. For example, in Wuyuan and Tunxi alone, there were originally over 300 tea factories, but in recent years, due to financial pressures, over 100 have ceased operations. Foreign sales have been shrinking daily. Farmers, unable to sell their tea leaves, have also abandoned tea fields to seek alternative livelihoods. Many tea-producing areas, due to their mountainous terrain, such as various counties in Huizhou and counties like Liuan, Yingshan, and Huoshan in northern Anhui, have suffered from bandit-communist devastation in recent years, leading to abandoned tea gardens. Furthermore, transportation in these mountainous counties is obstructed, making external transport inconvenient and further depressing the tea market. The following are methods for reorganizing and improving Anhui tea:

(I) Investigation: Investigate the tea-producing areas of various provinces and counties within the country, comparing the types of tea, values, and annual production quantities to understand the overall state of the tea industry. Items such as poor quality manufacturing and packaging should be investigated and improved upon at all times. As for tea-producing countries abroad, such as India, Ceylon, Java, and Japan, their tea varieties should also be investigated for their strengths and weaknesses. The superior ones should be purchased and propagated widely in tea-producing provinces and counties across the country for uniform improvement of planting. Other factors closely related to tea leaves, such as soil, geology, and climate, should also be carefully investigated and studied. Chinese tea distribution centers should be established in various commercial ports at home and abroad for both retail and wholesale, with the aim of expanding sales channels. Specialized investigators should also be established to specifically investigate the conditions of each sales channel and report to the government (province/county) at all times, which will then relay the information to various industrial organizations for transportation and broader sales.

(II) Guidance: Anhui Province has long enjoyed a reputation for tea production, but it lacks guidance. The tea industry is declining daily. In the future, more tea affairs training institutes should be established, enrolling a number of trainees to study specialized techniques. After graduation, they should be assigned to various tea-producing areas to guide farmers or jointly organize companies and cooperatives to improve and popularize tea, thus developing the future of the tea industry.

(III) Promotion: During each tea season, tea industry organizations (companies, cooperatives, agricultural experiment stations, agricultural science students, public education centers, farmer education centers, etc.) should send a number of lecturers to various tea-producing areas to promote methods of improving tea leaf planting, seeds, fertilization, and production. They should also contact various tea firms and tea merchants to discuss concrete measures for organizing tea production companies and purchasing machinery to fundamentally improve production. Jointly publish pamphlets, booklets, and various promotional leaflets, slogans, and advertisements to promote sales externally. Over time, this will become widespread, and the benefits will be substantial. In addition, the exquisite packaging of tea leaves and the beauty of trademarks can also be used to promote its advantages through text and images, thereby expanding sales.

(IV) Experimentation: Research and experimentation on tea affairs primarily involve seeds, fertilizers, soil, chemistry, climate, rainfall, insect pests, etc. However, given the current financial difficulties and the underdeveloped state of science, experimentation cannot be fully comprehensive. Priority should be given to indispensable experiments and research, such as nurseries, propagation, transplantation, pruning, strip sowing, row sowing, grafting, and other improved (scientific) production methods, following the steps of successful experiments in India.

(V) Improvement: (A) Chinese tea farmers generally do not pay attention to cultivation methods, or they simply use old methods. Tea planting in counties such as Liuan, Huoshan, and Shucheng in northern Anhui involves plowing and fertilizing only once a year, or sometimes neither plowing nor fertilizing, essentially treating the tea plants as if they were wild and not cultivated. The situation is similar in counties like Qimen, Wuyuan, and Qiupu in southern Anhui. Moreover, it is not easy to manage and cultivate in high mountainous areas, and nutrients in the soil are washed away by rain, leading to premature aging of tea trees and reduced leaf production. Therefore, tea gardens and tea industry organizations must pay attention to management. In sloping areas, strip sowing is recommended to suit tea tree growth, retain soil nutrients, and facilitate both work and management. Flat areas should be designated as nursery areas for transplantation and collection from other fields. (B) Only 2-3% of Chinese tea farmers use fertilizers. The fertilizers they use are generally human excrement, bean cake, oil cake, wood ash, compost, grass fertilizer, rice straw, etc. In Qimen County, rapeseed is grown everywhere for oil production, and the remaining residue, commonly known as "ku," is rich in protein and inexpensive, making it suitable for fertilizing tea trees. This method of fertilization should be widely promoted. (C) Production methods: Previously, the production of red and green tea relied solely on manual kneading. Now, reform and innovation are needed. Withering and fermentation of black tea using sunlight is not ideal because the heat is too intense, which can create a sunburned taste and lack of aroma when brewed with boiling water. Indoor withering should be adopted. The machinery used for green tea production is optimal, but due to economic difficulties, it is temporarily inconvenient to purchase. Imitate the original manual kneading method by steaming the leaves, then placing them on a cooling platform to reduce moisture slightly. Afterward, roast them with charcoal fire inside the kneading bed. After drying, the shape, color, aroma, and taste will be extremely beautiful. (D) Packaging: In northern Anhui, tea leaves are packed in bamboo baskets lined with cattail leaves, which is crude and unsatisfactory. Over time, the color, aroma, and taste will be greatly diminished. Although tea firms in southern Anhui use wooden boxes, they do not appeal to foreigners, and the box panels are too thin, often breaking during loading and unloading by customs. This creates inconvenience for foreign buyers. It is proposed to improve the packaging by producing colored iron bottles and cans in various sizes such as half a pound, one pound, five pounds, ten pounds, or in pounds, similar to canned food and biscuits today, to appeal to foreigners and facilitate transportation on travel vehicles and ships. For overseas exports, sturdy wooden boxes weighing fifty or one hundred pounds should be used for long-distance transportation and sales.

(VI) Promotion of Sales Channels: (A) Regularly publish surveys and statistics related to the tea industry, foreign preferences, trade conditions, financial situations, improvement strategies, and research findings, discussions, introductions, and critiques by experts, so that domestic tea merchants and tea farmers can learn from them. In addition, publishing specialized books and pamphlets can promote sales. (B) Contact tea merchants and tea firms in Beijing, Shanghai, Hankou, Fujian, Tianjin, Jinan, and other places to organize tea industry exchanges, cooperatives, and companies to form a complete sales plan. (C) Anhui tea producers lack knowledge of foreign languages and international trade, making it difficult for them to trade directly with foreigners. They have to rely on tea firms and listen to the instructions of interpreters, subject to the monopoly of foreign merchants and the deception of tea firms, resulting in unspeakable suffering. This also hinders the development of the tea industry. In the future, if distribution centers can be established in various foreign ports for retail and wholesale, with direct transportation and sales, the losses of tea merchants can be greatly reduced.

(VII) Steps for Reorganization: (A) Establish more planting and manufacturing branches or research institutions, hiring specialized personnel to provide guidance. (B) Organize a tea industry limited liability company for joint operation, developing the tea industry and expanding overseas and domestic commercial ports and markets. (C) Establish a tea industry bank or other financial institutions to circulate funds and activate the market. (D) Establish a tea industry inspection bureau to crack down on the production of substandard products and prevent unscrupulous merchants from mixing in inferior goods, which would damage foreign credibility. Promulgate regulations and strictly inspect to prevent unscrupulous merchants from engaging in fraud or manipulating the market. (E) Establish schools to cultivate specialized tea industry personnel, using research and practical methods to develop the future of the tea industry. (F) Raise funds to purchase machinery and scientifically improve tea production and manufacturing. (G) Manage tea gardens, eliminate pests, irrigate, and fertilize to increase production and improve tea quality. (H) Develop transportation to facilitate the transport of tea leaves. (End)

Shenbao Children's Supplement

Arise, Children! 156

— Chen Xijian

"They seem to think that children, besides eating and playing, understand nothing and can do nothing."

These are some words from the declaration of the Children's Travel Group of the Ten Children's Organizations in West Lake to the children. Yes, in people's minds, children simply give others this kind of impression, and are utterly incapable of anything else. However, because they could not bear this humiliation and ridicule, they "used facts to shatter this erroneous view of underestimating children." They came to Shanghai, earning their travel expenses through labor, without the leadership of teachers, and finally arrived safely in Shanghai. This heroic feat has shattered the humiliation suffered by tens of millions of children over thousands of years.

The purpose of their coming here is to see how imperialism oppresses the people of our semi-colonial countries and the people of all walks of life in Shanghai. This is so brave and worthy of praise!

Dear children! Living in such a city, witnessing the oppression of imperialism and the different characters of all walks of life, what are your feelings? Do you feel sad? You eat your father's food, use your father's money to study, and still rely on your father to see movies, eat candy, and play with toys. Do you feel sad or happy? Can you endure this enormous humiliation?

I hope that you will also "unite" like the ten children in Hangzhou and "show our strength to do something for them to see, so that they will no longer underestimate us in the future."

Children! Arise! Don't lie in your mother's arms, living that sweet (?) life! Know that although candy is very sweet, in the end, it always leaves a slightly sour and unpleasant taste in your mouth. Let you rise and shatter this erroneous concept!

Modern American Prodigy 157

— Da Zhai

This child's name is Martin. He lives in Austin, Texas, USA. He is only ten years old this year and was admitted to Austin High School in the summer of the year before last. He is expected to enter the University of Texas next year.

His talent is especially intelligent. Before the age of two, he could read short English sentences. At the age of three, he could clearly remember the names of the borders between the states of the United States. At the age of four, he was able to study astronomy and geography on his own with very good results. At the age of five, he entered a private middle school in Austin. In two years, he skipped to junior high school, and in another two years, he skipped to high school again.

His reading speed is an average of 1,600 words per minute. At his fastest reading speed, he can read 2,100 words per minute, as tested by the "scientific eye" method at his school.

From this scientific eye, it was also discovered that the reason why Martin can read so quickly is that when he reads the first line, his eyes are already slanted to the left, looking at the second and third lines... continuing to look down. This perfectly fits the saying "reading ten lines at a glance," which is impossible for ordinary people.

Generally, those who are extremely intelligent are often unwilling to study hard, but Martin makes studying his only hobby. Also, it is difficult to understand when reading too quickly, but Martin's memory is not weak after reading, and he can speak very clearly and thoughtfully when telling others about it. There are also people who are intelligent and willing to study hard, but do not like sports and are often physically weak, but Martin loves sports very much. He likes horse riding and swimming the most, so his body is very strong. He weighs 90 pounds and is four feet eight inches tall, looking like he is thirteen years old.

Martin is particularly intelligent, which is difficult for ordinary people to force, but his hard work and training of his body can be done by all children!

Cod Liver Oil 159

— Zhen

"Min'er, your body is not very strong, how can you serve the country in the future? So you must always pay attention to exercise, exercise is the only way to build a strong body, but don't be too strenuous, just one hour of exercise a day is enough. On the one hand, eat some supplements, this is the so-called external cultivation and internal nourishment, and your body will naturally become strong." Min'er's father always told him this. So one afternoon, he bought a bottle of cod liver oil back. Min'er felt that the cod liver oil was fishy and unpalatable, so he didn't want to eat it, but in order to strengthen his body, he had to reluctantly eat it. He didn't understand why his father gave him something that didn't taste good?

"Dad, why don't you give me something delicious to eat, but you insist on giving me this unpalatable cod liver oil? What are the benefits of cod liver oil?"

"There is a substance in our lives that is indispensable, that is, vitamin, also called life element. This substance was first discovered in rice and milk, but the quantity is very small, and there is relatively more in cod liver oil. If we lack this vitamin, we will not be able to avoid becoming weak and unhealthy."

"What is this cod liver oil made of?"

"Cod liver oil is made from a kind of sea fish in the Pacific and Atlantic Oceans. This sea fish is called the cod, which is produced in the northern Pacific and Atlantic Oceans. This cod is large and small. The large ones average about twenty to thirty pounds, which is about fifteen to twenty catties in our country. The small ones are also twelve pounds. You can know the size and shape of the fish by looking at the picture on the cod liver oil bottle. It is 150 to 500 feet below the seabed, so catching the cod is not easy. Cod is rich in fat, and cod liver oil is extracted from it. Its meat can also be eaten, fresh, pickled, or dried, but this fish is not sold in our country's markets.

"The countries that operate this fishery include England, France, the United States, Japan, and Newfoundland. The coastal area of Newfoundland (in North America) produces more fish, so in 1713 AD, England made Newfoundland a colony."

Five-Minute Fairytale 160

— He Gongchao

Treasure in the Well

A merchant was carrying many pearls and treasures, walking at night, and accidentally fell into a dry well. This well was more than ten feet deep. It was more difficult to climb out than to ascend to heaven. So he was anxious and sweating, shouting, "Help! Help!"

Four or five people nearby heard his shouts and ran over. But one of the most powerful people drew out a knife and pointed at the other three or four people, saying, "I'll save him, you're not allowed to save him! He is my cousin, only I can save him, get out!"

The others, seeing him so fierce, stood aside and watched for the time being. So he leaned over to the well and said to the man in the well, "Look, those people just now were robbers trying to steal your things. They didn't really come to save you. Now, I'm here to save you." As he spoke, he took a rope and dropped it down from above. The man in the well thought that the savior had really come, and hurriedly grabbed the rope, wrapped it around his waist, hoping that the people above would pull him up immediately.

Unexpectedly, the man shouted, "Wait a minute, first hang your pearls and treasures up, and I'll keep them for you. There are many robbers here, and you don't have the strength to deal with them!" The man in the well didn't think it over carefully, and in confusion, listened to his words, tied the pearls and treasures to the rope, and hung them up. The man got the pearls and treasures, took a large stone, and with a "smash," as if Mount Tai was pressing down, the poor stupid merchant was crushed flat.

The man went home with the stolen goods in a state of elation, but the people who had been watching just now suddenly came out to stop him and shouted, "Hey, friend, know what's good for you! Let's share the benefits, don't swallow them all!" So, this group of people all showed fierce faces and started fighting, each trying to grab the merchant's things.

The Kidnapped Child

The Zhang family had a child who was very smart and handsome, but the Li family next door took a fancy to him. One night, the Li family actually sent a few servants to break into the child's bedroom and carry him away. They insisted on changing his name and acknowledging them as his father. The Zhang family was not as powerful as the Li family and refused to cheer up, bearing the humiliation silently. The child lived in the Li family, suffering oppression and pain. Although the father and son lived apart, they always missed each other day and night in their hearts. The son thought in his heart, "Dad, although I have been robbed now, sooner or later, I will return to your arms." The father thought in his heart, "Poor child, I am really sorry for you, because I am useless and make you suffer like this. However, I will never forget you, and I will get you back one day."

However, things in the world are really infuriating: before the wishes of this unfortunate father and son could be realized, the powerful Li family had already taken further action. One day, he took a knife and ran to the Zhang family, saying fiercely to the Zhang family, "This child is mine now. From now on, his surname is Li, and I am in charge of all his affairs. You are not allowed to interfere. If you don't acknowledge him as his father, I want you to acknowledge this matter. If you acknowledge my words later, please take this knife first!"

Springtime Life 162

— Dong You

Scientific Trivia

Is the Air Fresh in the Woods in the Morning? 163

— Zi Xi

Everyone knows that people cannot breathe in polluted air and must breathe in fresh air often. In fact, the so-called pollution of air is just that there is too much carbonic acid gas in the air: the so-called freshness is just that there is less carbonic acid gas in the air. It is harmful to breathe in polluted air and beneficial to breathe in fresh air. Many people think that the air in the woods in the morning is very fresh and that breathing it in is very beneficial to the body. But this view is not entirely correct. Because plants perform a photochemical reaction during the day, absorbing carbon dioxide and releasing oxygen; at night, they perform a respiratory reaction, absorbing oxygen and releasing carbon dioxide. Therefore, in the woods in the morning, the photochemical reaction has not yet prevailed, and the carbonic acid gas released during the respiratory reaction last night is still stored in the woods. So, can the air in the woods in the morning be considered fresh? But, as long as the prevailing photochemical reaction has passed, it will be very fresh and clean. So it is important for children not to go to the woods too early to breathe.

What Kind of Person Will I Be in the Future? 164

— Yang Jingzhen, Wuxi County Central Elementary School

(Eleventh Place)

The modern world—the world of the twentieth century, is a world of science. In the world of science, there must be a scientific China. Who will create a scientific China? It is up to the children of China to create it. So, what kind of children should the children of China be? They should be scientific children.

In the past, I was an ignorant child, living a life of amusement in a hazy way. Since I read Tao Xingzhi's "How to Be a Scientific Child," it startled my hazy mind and made me realize that I must work hard and serve society in the future. I must never waste the most precious period of my life—my student days.

I hope that I will be a person like Franklin Watt in the future, creating many scientific instruments to supply China to fight against the enemy, recover the four northeastern provinces, abolish all unequal treaties, and raise China's international status, and also become a strong country, standing side by side with the Central American countries in the world, and doing my best to rescue weak nations and resist violence, to create myself into a scientific person, with a union of hands and brain, with no fear, to conquer all of nature.

The Tale of a Loyal Dog (14) 165

— Xin Qing

The old Red Mill, which he originally considered his sole destination, was a place he frequented. He would always stop in front of the mill, where a little girl with a cloud of curly hair would peek out to welcome him. In her rosy little hands, she often held a bone or a piece of hard bread for Baderxi to eat.

Now, every time they passed, Baderxi would look with disappointment at the closed door, and Xiao Fuluo no longer stopped in front of it. His heart filled with bitterness, he hurried past. Poor little Ailuo in the house sat on a small stool by the fireplace, tears streaming down her face, dampening the knitting in her hands. Her father, Kegangshi, worked beside the millstone and flour sacks, his resolve unchanged, secretly saying to himself, "This is for the best! That child always thinks about useless things; he's destined to be a beggar. If I let them stay together, who knows what troubles it will cause in the future!"

Although Xiao Nanluo was treated coldly like this, he didn't complain, because he was naturally quiet. His grandfather, old Dashi, had often told him, "We are poor people, and we must submit to God's will in all things. Whether we receive good or bad, we should accept it, because the poor cannot choose."

Xiao Nanluo listened quietly to these words, because he respected his old grandfather very much. However, he was a gifted child, so a sweet and uncertain hope whispered in his heart, "But the poor can sometimes choose—choose to become a great person, and no one can say they are wrong."

He always thought about it silently. One day, Xiao Ailuo accidentally bumped into him in the rice fields by the canal. She ran to his side and hugged him, sobbing sadly, because tomorrow was her name day, and her parents were preparing a celebratory feast, but they weren't inviting Xiao Nanluo to participate, which made her sad and tearful. Xiao Nanluo kissed her and said to her quietly with great confidence, "Ailuo, things will change one day. The piece of pine board that your father brought back will be as valuable as silver. He won't keep me out then. Just always love me, dear Ailuo; just always love me, and I will definitely become a great person."

Xiao Ailuo asked through teary eyes, "What if I don't love you?"

Xiao Nanluo's eyes left her face and looked far away, straight to the spire of the Great Mosque illuminated by the golden-red setting sun. A sweet and melancholic smile appeared on his face, which startled Xiao Ailuo. He burst out a firm word in his breath, "I will eventually become a great person, Ailuo. If I don't, I might as well die."

Xiao Ailuo pushed him away, pouting, and said, "Then you don't love me." Xiao Nanluo shook his head, smiled slightly, and walked away triumphantly through the yellow straw. A vision seemed to appear before him, a splendid future, as if he had returned to his hometown in high spirits, proposing marriage to Xiao Ailuo's parents.
